padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; widows: 1; line-height: 30px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n		<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">　　虾是最受欢迎的水产类食品，也是维生素</span>D的主要饮食来源之一。90克虾能提供每日所需维生素D的30%，高于一杯牛奶的维生素D含量。</span></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 9px 0px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; widows: 1; line-height: 30px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n		<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">　　虾是最受欢迎的水产类食品，也是维生素</span>D的主要饮食来源之一。90克虾能提供每日所需维生素D的30%，高于一杯牛奶的维生素D含量。</span></p>\r\n	<p style=\"margin: 9px 0px 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">腰椎间盘突出症简称腰突症，是一种常见病，表现为坐骨神经痛</span>--病人一侧腰部疼痛，经臀部向大腿后方放射(串痛)，直到小腿和足部，并伴有麻木。&nbsp;</span><br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" />\r\n	<br style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\" />\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; color: rgb(0, 0, 0); letter-spacing: 0px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">　　椎间盘位于椎体之间，像一个小圆饼。四周是富有弹性和韧性的纤维环，中央的</span>&ldquo;馅&rdquo;是&ldquo;髓核&rdquo;。椎间盘缺少直接血液营养供应，活动度大，又负担人体80%的重量，因此髓核于20岁、纤维环于30岁以后即开始老化(退变)，弹性和抗压能力下降。在此基础上，腰部活动姿势不当或用力过猛，纤维环后部可由里向外产生裂隙，导致髓核组织突出或脱出，压迫后方神经根，引起症状。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">与中老年人不同，</span>20岁以下的青少年椎间盘尚未开始退变。因此，青少年腰突症多由剧烈体力活动时受伤诱发。腰椎在负荷并快速旋转时，间盘纤维环最易造成破坏。此外，与先天性椎管狭窄、腰椎侧弯、腰骶部移行椎等先天发育异常也有一定关系。&nbsp;</span><br style=\"margin: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">　　1.工作姿势：社会在进步，人们的工作形势也逐渐在发生变化，如今越来越多的白领和电脑工作者，开始长时间坐在电脑前工作，且不能够保持正确的坐姿.专家提醒，不良坐姿会使腰部屈曲，腰椎间盘受到压迫，极易引发腰椎间盘病变。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 20px 0px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; widows: 1; text-indent: 32px; line-height: 28px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2.腰部负荷过大：如果长期从事劳累过度的工作，经常腰部超负荷，如装卸工，经常提举重物，迫使腰椎间盘长久处于过度负荷状态，纤维环破裂，引发突出。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; font-size: 16px; font-variant-numeric: normal; font-variant-east-asian: normal; line-height: 25.6px; widows: 1; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">\r\n	<span style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; font-family: 微软雅黑; color: rgb(47, 47, 47); letter-spacing: 0px; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">御衙宁骨肌康，比较有用它是结合百年传承的配方和新型科技的体现，因为配方是三百多年的传承下来的所以又被誉为非遗，纯天然大自然的馈赠。对九五成以上的人都是起到不错的作用，如果严重可以试一下。</span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 20px 0px 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; clear: both; min-height: 1em; color: rgb(62, 62, 62); font-family: &quot;Helvetica Neue&quot;, Helvetica, &quot;Hiragino Sans GB&quot;, &quot;Microsoft YaHei&quot;, Arial, sans-serif; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; font-family: Helvetica; color: rgb(51, 51, 51); letter-spacing: 0px; font-size: 18px;\">1、处方：核桃仁210克、黑芝麻210克、杜仲60克、川续断30克、木瓜30克、菟丝子60克、当归60克。<img _src=\"http://s15.sinaimg.cn/mw690/006BRIH9zy76eithWYS2e&amp;690\" alt=\"\" data-ratio=\"0.66796875\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://s15.sinaimg.cn/mw690/006BRIH9zy76eithWYS2e&amp;690\" style=\"margin: 0px; padding: 0px; max-width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important;\">除核桃仁、黑芝麻外，余药均晒干，研磨过筛备用。将黑芝麻于碾槽内碾碎，再放入核桃仁一起碾，当用手摸无颗粒时，与经过筛的药面一起倒入盆中，以炼蜜</span>250克分数次加入盆内搅拌，反复揉搓成团块,再取团块7克制成丸子。丸子可放入冰箱内贮存。每日服2次，每次服一丸，黄酒20毫克送下。连服100丸为一疗程。 </span></p>\r\n<p style=\"margin: 20px 0px 0px;
